<script>function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
  if (!cookieName || document.cookie.indexOf(cookieName) === -1) {
    return undefined;
  }

  try {
    var cookieArray = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^| )".concat(cookieName, "=([^;]+)")));

    if (cookieArray && cookieArray.length > 0) {
      return decodeURIComponent(cookieArray.pop());
    }

    return undefined;
  } catch (e) {
    return undefined;
  }
}; function getCustomerNameAndGreeting() {
  var isSignedIn = getCookieValue("hasCID") === "1";
  var customer = getCookieValue("customer");

  if (isSignedIn && customer && customer.length) {
    try {
      customer = JSON.parse(customer);

      if (customer.firstName) {
        return "Hi, ".concat(customer.firstName, " ").concat(customer.lastNameInitial);
      }

      return undefined;
    } catch (e) {
      return undefined;
    }
  }

  return undefined;
}; function replaceAccountSubLinkText() {
  var customerNameAndGreeting = getCustomerNameAndGreeting();
  var accountSubText = document.querySelector("#signIn");

  if (customerNameAndGreeting && accountSubText) {
    accountSubText.textContent = customerNameAndGreeting;
  }
};
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () { 
      try{
        replaceAccountSubLinkText();
      } catch(e) {console.log("Error in glass-hf client code", e)}
    });
</script>

data-tl-id="categorypage-SEOCustomHTML"><div class="SeoCustomHtml-data"><h2>ATV &amp; Off-Road</h2>
<p>Gear up and get ready to go out on an off-road adventure. Whether you're taking your ATV or dune buggy out to the desert or your snowmobile out on the slopes, Walmart.com has a wide variety of accessories and parts to suit your riding style at Every Day Low Prices.</p>
<h3>What are some popular off-road accessories?</h3>
<p>
</p><ul><li><b>Helmets and riding gear:</b> Waterproof body armor can help protect you from injuries or inclement weather while you ride. Mesh and textile jackets and pants can help keep you cool when it's hot, while leather gear and gloves can keep you warm and dry in the mud and snow. Protective goggles are another off-road essential. They can protect your eyes from dirt and dust or prevent trees and branches from hitting you in the face. You can find a wide variety of protective jackets, gloves, body armor, goggles and boots from brands like Alpinestars, O'Neal Racing, Castle-X, Troy Lee Designs, Fly Racing and 100%.</li>
<li><b>ATV and UTV tires:</b> For your safety, it's important to check your tires before every ride. If you can see the tread wear indicators, it's time to replace them. At Walmart, you can find a variety of off-road tires and replacement parts from brands like Goodyear, Bridgestone and Continental.</li>
<b>Parts and accessories:</b> Whether it's powersport batteries or ATV and UTV covers, you can find all the accessories you need to keep your all-terrain vehicle in tip-top shape. You can also find an assortment of cargo bags to hold onto your essential items while you're on the move.</ul>
<p></p>

  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch && sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj && typeof obj === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function(k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  }

  function getAppName() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.applicationName", window);
  }

    return get("_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.midasConfig", window) || {};

    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  }

  window._wml.adLoader = (function() {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        addPerfMark('fire-event-' + eventName);
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function(listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      },
    };
  })();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent("instant"); // Default load ads immediately
})();
